Moves the fifth leg to the top of an obstacle. 

Moves the fifth leg to the top of an obstacle and moves the robot forwards.

\index{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}!First\+\_\+\+Leg@{First\+\_\+\+Leg}}
\index{First\+\_\+\+Leg@{First\+\_\+\+Leg}!over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{First\+\_\+\+Leg(char direction)}{First_Leg(char direction)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void First\+\_\+\+Leg (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char}]{direction}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{over__hinder_8c_a8e93e827f047dac258e8334869fb2615}{}\label{over__hinder_8c_a8e93e827f047dac258e8334869fb2615}


Moves the first leg to the top of an obstacle. 

Moves the first leg to the top of an obstacle and moves the robot forwards. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source_l00194}{194} of file \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source}{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}.

\index{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}!Fourth\+\_\+\+Leg@{Fourth\+\_\+\+Leg}}
\index{Fourth\+\_\+\+Leg@{Fourth\+\_\+\+Leg}!over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Fourth\+\_\+\+Leg(char direction)}{Fourth_Leg(char direction)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Fourth\+\_\+\+Leg (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char}]{direction}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{over__hinder_8c_aa7388d904fc9be082274a66dcb366d34}{}\label{over__hinder_8c_aa7388d904fc9be082274a66dcb366d34}


Moves the fourth leg to the top of an obstacle. 

Moves the fourth leg to the top of an obstacle and moves the robot forwards. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source_l00446}{446} of file \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source}{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}.

\index{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}!Second\+\_\+\+Leg@{Second\+\_\+\+Leg}}
\index{Second\+\_\+\+Leg@{Second\+\_\+\+Leg}!over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Second\+\_\+\+Leg(char direction)}{Second_Leg(char direction)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Second\+\_\+\+Leg (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char}]{direction}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{over__hinder_8c_a656636b54d65528c5f66fbe1ae0c793c}{}\label{over__hinder_8c_a656636b54d65528c5f66fbe1ae0c793c}


Moves the second leg to the top of an obstacle. 

Moves the second leg to the top of an obstacle and moves the robot forwards. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source_l00275}{275} of file \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source}{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}.

Moves the sixth leg to the top of an obstacle. 

Moves the sixth leg to the top of an obstacle and moves the robot forwards.

\index{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}!Third\+\_\+\+Leg@{Third\+\_\+\+Leg}}
\index{Third\+\_\+\+Leg@{Third\+\_\+\+Leg}!over\+\_\+hinder.\+c@{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Third\+\_\+\+Leg(char direction)}{Third_Leg(char direction)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Third\+\_\+\+Leg (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char}]{direction}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{over__hinder_8c_ae5a0956265d1177bb332cba019226908}{}\label{over__hinder_8c_ae5a0956265d1177bb332cba019226908}


Moves the third leg to the top of an obstacle. 

Moves the third leg to the top of an obstacle and moves the robot forwards. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source_l00369}{369} of file \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_source}{over\+\_\+hinder.\+c}.

Keeps track on the lenght previous step. 

The lenght of the previous steps in a climb is needed for making the following steps smooth.

\end{DoxyParams}

Makes the robot climb an obstacle of the height 6.\+5 cm. 

A sereis of hardcoded movements for acending a step with the height 6.\+5 cm
